CREATE TABLE customers (
    customerNumber INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    contactFirstName VARCHAR(50),
    contactLastName VARCHAR(50),
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    addressLine1 VARCHAR(255),
    addressLine2 VARCHAR(255),
    city VARCHAR(100),
    state VARCHAR(50),
    postalCode VARCHAR(20),
    country VARCHAR(50),
    salesRepEmployeeNumber INT,
    score INT DEFAULT 0,
    creditLimit INT DEFAULT 0,
    Rating_of_experience INT
);



CREATE TABLE customers_data (
    CustomerNumber INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    Prefix VARCHAR(10),
    FirstName VARCHAR(50),
    LastName VARCHAR(50),
    BirthDate DATE,
    MaritalStatus CHAR(1),
    Gender CHAR(1),
    EmailAddress VARCHAR(100),
    Password VARCHAR(50),
    AnnualIncome VARCHAR(20),
    TotalChildren INT,
    EducationLevel VARCHAR(50),
    Occupation VARCHAR(50),
    HomeOwner CHAR(1),
    CustomersProfilePhoto BLOB,
    CustomersExperienceReview INT
FOREIGN KEY (CustomerNumber) REFERENCES customers(customerNumber)
);




CREATE TABLE CustomersReviewImages (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    img_url VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    prd_code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
EmailAddress VARCHAR(100)
);



CREATE TABLE employees (
    employeeNumber INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    lastName VARCHAR(50),
    firstName VARCHAR(50),
    extension VARCHAR(10),
    email VARCHAR(100),
    officeCode INT,
    reportsTo INT,
    jobTitle VARCHAR(50)
);



CREATE TABLE images_table (
    id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    img_url VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    img_txt TEXT NOT NULL
);





CREATE TABLE offices (
    officeCode INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    city VARCHAR(100),
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    addressLine1 VARCHAR(255),
    addressLine2 VARCHAR(255),
    state VARCHAR(50),
    country VARCHAR(50),
    postalCode VARCHAR(20),
    territory VARCHAR(50)
);








CREATE TABLE payments (
    checkNumber VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    customerNumber INT,
    paymentDate DATE,
    amount DECIMAL(10,2),
FOREIGN KEY (customerNumber) REFERENCES customers(customerNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE
);





CREATE TABLE products (
    productCode VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    productName VARCHAR(255),
    productLine VARCHAR(200),
    productVendor VARCHAR(100),
    productDescription TEXT,
    quantityInStock INT,
    buyPrice DECIMAL(10,2),
    MSRP DECIMAL(10,2),
    mainProductImage BLOB
);




CREATE TABLE product_files (
    file_Id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    product_Code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    color VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    file_src TEXT NOT NULL,
    Quantity_Pack INT DEFAULT 1,
    Quantity_Pack_Price INT DEFAULT 0,
    Quantity_Pack_Name VARCHAR(500),
FOREIGN KEY (product_Code) REFERENCES products(productCode) ON DELETE CASCADE

  
);





CREATE TABLE returned_ordered_products (
    returnId INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    returned_Date DATE NOT NULL,
    return_Issue VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    return_Description TEXT,
    orderNumber INT NOT NULL,
    productCode VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    CustomerNumber INT NOT NULL,
    Return_Success TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0
);




CREATE TABLE returns (
    returnId INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    orderNumber INT,
    productCode VARCHAR(50),
    returnDate DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    returnReason ENUM('quality_issue','damaged','part_missing','wrong_item','size_issue','color_issue'),
    returnOption ENUM('return','replace','refund'),
    description TEXT,
    photoPath VARCHAR(255),
    status ENUM('return_placed','pickup_scheduled','picked_up','return_processed','refund_processed','replacement_sent'),
    customerId INT,
FOREIGN KEY (orderNumber) REFERENCES orders(orderNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE
);



CREATE TABLE cartplaceorder (
    cartPlaceOrderNum INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    customerNumber INT,
    orderNumber INT,
    orderNumberCart INT,
    productCode VARCHAR(50),
    colorMainImage BLOB,
    quantityOrdered INT,
    productSize VARCHAR(50),
    priceEach DECIMAL(10,2),
    totalCost DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (quantityOrdered * priceEach) STORED,
    amountReceived DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
    amountPending DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (totalCost - amountReceived) STORED,
    modeOfPayment VARCHAR(50),
    orderLineNumber INT,
    orderDate DATE,
    requiredDate DATE,
    shippedDate DATE,
    status VARCHAR(20),
    ratingOfStars INT,
    comments TEXT,
FOREIGN KEY (orderNumber) REFERENCES orders(orderNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (productCode) REFERENCES products(productCode) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (customerNumber) REFERENCES customers(customerNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE

);





CREATE TABLE orders (
    orderNumber INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    orderDate DATE,
    requiredDate DATE,
    shippedDate DATE,
    status VARCHAR(20),
    ratingOfStars INT,
    customerNumber INT,
    comments TEXT
);



CREATE TABLE order_details (
    orderNumber INT NOT NULL,
    productCode VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    quantityOrdered INT,
    priceEach DECIMAL(10,2),
    orderLineNumber INT,
    totalCost DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (quantityOrdered * priceEach) STORED,
    amountReceived DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
    amountPending DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (totalCost - amountReceived) STORED,
    productSize VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'free size',
    modeOfPayment VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT 'cart',
    colorMainImage BLOB,
    PRIMARY KEY (orderNumber, productCode)
FOREIGN KEY (orderNumber) REFERENCES orders(orderNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  FOREIGN KEY (productCode) REFERENCES products(productCode) ON DELETE CASCADE
);

To resolve the "The MySQL server is running with the --secure-file-priv option" error, you need to either disable secure_file_priv or move your files to the directory specified by this variable. 
1. Check the current setting:
Open your MySQL command-line client and run SHOW VARIABLES LIKE "secure_file_priv"; to see the current directory configured for secure_file_priv. 
2. Option 1: Disable secure_file_priv:
Edit the MySQL configuration file: Locate the my.cnf (or my.ini on Windows) file. This file is typically found in /etc/mysql/ or /etc/my.cnf.d/ (or the equivalent on Windows). 
Find the secure_file_priv setting: Look for a line that defines secure_file_priv.
Set it to an empty string: Change the value to secure_file_priv = ''. 
Save the changes.
Stop and restart the MySQL server: Use commands like sudo service mysql stop and sudo service mysql start (or the equivalent on your system). 
3. Option 2: Move your files:
Move your files to the directory specified by secure_file_priv: If you are loading or importing files, move them to the directory shown by SHOW VARIABLES LIKE "secure_file_priv";. 
4. Using LOAD DATA INFILE with secure_file_priv (if you can't disable it):
Ensure the files are in the allowed directory:
Make sure the files you're using with LOAD DATA INFILE are located within the directory specified by secure_file_priv. 
Grant appropriate privileges:
The MySQL user you're using must have the FILE privilege to access files in that directory.

sql

FIELDS TERMINATED BY ','

Final Code:




CREATE TABLE customers (
    customerNumber INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    contactFirstName VARCHAR(50),
    contactLastName VARCHAR(50),
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    addressLine1 VARCHAR(255),
    addressLine2 VARCHAR(255),
    city VARCHAR(100),
    state VARCHAR(50),
    postalCode VARCHAR(20),
    country VARCHAR(50),
    salesRepEmployeeNumber INT,
    score INT DEFAULT 0,
    creditLimit INT DEFAULT 0,
    Rating_of_experience INT
);



CREATE TABLE customers_data (
    CustomerNumber INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    Prefix VARCHAR(10),
    FirstName VARCHAR(50),
    LastName VARCHAR(50),
    BirthDate DATE,
    MaritalStatus CHAR(1),
    Gender CHAR(1),
    EmailAddress VARCHAR(100),
    Password VARCHAR(50),
    AnnualIncome VARCHAR(20),
    TotalChildren INT,
    EducationLevel VARCHAR(50),
    Occupation VARCHAR(50),
    HomeOwner CHAR(1),
    CustomersProfilePhoto BLOB,
    CustomersExperienceReview INT,
FOREIGN KEY (CustomerNumber) REFERENCES customers(customerNumber)
);




CREATE TABLE CustomersReviewImages (
    id INT AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    img_url VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    prd_code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
EmailAddress VARCHAR(100)
);



CREATE TABLE employees (
    employeeNumber INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    lastName VARCHAR(50),
    firstName VARCHAR(50),
    extension VARCHAR(10),
    email VARCHAR(100),
    officeCode INT,
    reportsTo INT,
    jobTitle VARCHAR(50)
);



CREATE TABLE images_table (
    id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    img_url VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    img_txt TEXT NOT NULL
);





CREATE TABLE offices (
    officeCode INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    city VARCHAR(100),
    phone VARCHAR(20),
    addressLine1 VARCHAR(255),
    addressLine2 VARCHAR(255),
    state VARCHAR(50),
    country VARCHAR(50),
    postalCode VARCHAR(20),
    territory VARCHAR(50)
);








CREATE TABLE payments (
    checkNumber VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    customerNumber INT,
    paymentDate DATE,
    amount DECIMAL(10,2),
FOREIGN KEY (customerNumber) REFERENCES customers(customerNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE
);





CREATE TABLE products (
    productCode VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    productName VARCHAR(255),
    productLine VARCHAR(200),
    productVendor VARCHAR(100),
    productDescription TEXT,
    quantityInStock INT,
    buyPrice DECIMAL(10,2),
    MSRP DECIMAL(10,2),
    mainProductImage BLOB
);




CREATE TABLE product_files (
    file_Id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    product_Code VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    color VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    file_src TEXT NOT NULL,
    Quantity_Pack INT DEFAULT 1,
    Quantity_Pack_Price INT DEFAULT 0,
    Quantity_Pack_Name VARCHAR(500),
FOREIGN KEY (product_Code) REFERENCES products(productCode) ON DELETE CASCADE);





CREATE TABLE returned_ordered_products (
    returnId INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    returned_Date DATE NOT NULL,
    return_Issue VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    return_Description TEXT,
    orderNumber INT NOT NULL,
    productCode VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    CustomerNumber INT NOT NULL,
    Return_Success TINYINT(1) DEFAULT 0
);




CREATE TABLE returns (
    returnId INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    orderNumber INT,
    productCode VARCHAR(50),
    returnDate DATETIME DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    returnReason ENUM('quality_issue','damaged','part_missing','wrong_item','size_issue','color_issue'),
    returnOption ENUM('return','replace','refund'),
    description TEXT,
    photoPath VARCHAR(255),
    status ENUM('return_placed','pickup_scheduled','picked_up','return_processed','refund_processed','replacement_sent'),
    customerId INT,
FOREIGN KEY (orderNumber) REFERENCES orders(orderNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE
);



CREATE TABLE orders (
    orderNumber INT NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    orderDate DATE,
    requiredDate DATE,
    shippedDate DATE,
    status VARCHAR(20),
    ratingOfStars INT,
    customerNumber INT,
    comments TEXT
);



CREATE TABLE order_details (
    orderNumber INT NOT NULL,
    productCode VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    quantityOrdered INT,
    priceEach DECIMAL(10,2),
    orderLineNumber INT,
    totalCost DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (quantityOrdered * priceEach) STORED,
    amountReceived DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
    amountPending DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (totalCost - amountReceived) STORED,
    productSize VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'free size',
    modeOfPayment VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT 'cart',
    colorMainImage BLOB,
    PRIMARY KEY (orderNumber, productCode),
    FOREIGN KEY (orderNumber) REFERENCES orders(orderNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (productCode) REFERENCES products(productCode) ON DELETE CASCADE
);




CREATE TABLE cartplaceorder (
    cartPlaceOrderNum INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT PRIMARY KEY,
    customerNumber INT,
    orderNumber INT,
    orderNumberCart INT,
    productCode VARCHAR(50),
    colorMainImage BLOB,
    quantityOrdered INT,
    productSize VARCHAR(50),
    priceEach DECIMAL(10,2),
    totalCost DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (quantityOrdered * priceEach) STORED,
    amountReceived DECIMAL(10,2) DEFAULT 0.00,
    amountPending DECIMAL(10,2) GENERATED ALWAYS AS (totalCost - amountReceived) STORED,
    modeOfPayment VARCHAR(50),
    orderLineNumber INT,
    orderDate DATE,
    requiredDate DATE,
    shippedDate DATE,
    status VARCHAR(20),
    ratingOfStars INT,
    comments TEXT,
FOREIGN KEY (orderNumber) REFERENCES orders(orderNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (productCode) REFERENCES products(productCode) ON DELETE CASCADE,
    FOREIGN KEY (customerNumber) REFERENCES customers(customerNumber) ON DELETE CASCADE);
